< Text>
I don't even know where to begin! We originally came to the area to "take a look" at another nursery nearby, but found out about this one on Google, so we figured we'd give it a try. Holy moly am I glad we did!

To start off, Navarro was extremely friendly and welcoming upon entrance. We was very helpful with several of our questions, showed us several options that would fit our hot central valley climate, and told us how to care for the plants we already have that are hurting a little bit.

As far as the plants go, there is such a large variety of plants, that are both rare and some extremely large, that it felt like we were walking through a succulent museum!  The prices were very good for the condition and size of plants you can buy.

Our trip that started out as "just looking" ended up with us spending $250 on a bunch of absolutely gorgeous plants! We will definitely be making the two hour drive when we are ready for more plants!<//Text>

< review>
If you want to see the largest echeveria you've ever seen in your life you must stop here!  Really nice selection of succulents and cacti, a good mix of common varieties and rare plants.  If you're after rare plants don't come here expecting a bargain, the prices are fairly standard for what you'll see at other places.  However, this is one of the few places that has these plants in stock, so if you prefer buying in person rather than over the internet you'll have a good time.  The more common varieties are fairly priced and you can find some large specimens.  The owner is very friendly and enjoys talking plants, so chat him up if you want some growing tips.  He does some of his own cross breeding of echeveria and has made some really interesting (and massive) plants, they're super cool!</review>

<rating>5<//rating>< Review>
My friends and I came in here for Brunch on a Sunday.  We were immediately impressed by how open the space is.  It's nice to eat and not feel like people are all around you, plenty of space.  The Brunch Menu was pretty interesting, and I'd go back for it again.  The beer menu was kind of amazing, and is probably worth a trip on it's own.

For Food, I got a sandwich modeled after a Montecristo, the whole thing was deep fried.  Everyone at the table tried it and loved it!  Worth it for sure.  I also got a side of their Tater Tots, just plain ones.  But they were well cooked and lightly salted.  Good stuff.

Everyone else seemed to enjoy their food as well.  Definitely heading back and hopefully trying their standard menu, cause it looked amazing.</Review>

Most recently I had the Meatless Wonder veggie burger, which is something they make using fresh ingredients, rather than the mass-produced veggie burger patty you might expect from most places. < date>
1501545612325<//date>
<Rating>2< /Rating>< Text>
This place is about the beer, that's it. As I don't care about beer this is about the food and service. My opinion after having lunch there thee times. Two different burgers and a pizza. Let's start with the pizza, not much more than something you would find in the frozen food section of Save Mart. Sour dough thin crust, not very sour by the way, with a light layer of cheese and a sparse topping. Not much to it, not a lot of flavor and over priced and only comes in one size.  Not sure of reasons but if you order pizza plan on 45 to 60 minutes before it gets to your table, to slow for any body with only an hour for lunch. Let's move on to the burgers, there is a few to choose from I've tried two different ones. For a coke and burger plan on spend about $15 plus tip. The burgers only come with tots, yes tots like got as a kid in the school cafeteria. So if you like tots your set, I don't nor do I want to be reminded of tots on a cafeteria tray. Yep it even comes with a tray, if you'd rather have something else than tots for $3 more you can have small plan salad. That's enough about the tater tots, let's talk about the burgers themselves. In a single world average, better burgers to be had elsewhere in downtown Modesto for the same or less money. The service seams to run on the slow side. Don't plan on having your glass refilled, but there is soda dispenser in the back if you get tired of waiting for that refill. Also the place is very very noisy, bad place for a business lunch or to have a conversation at a reasonable voice level. If you are just interested beers this may be the place for you, otherwise better places for lunch in downtown Modesto for the money.</Text>

<Name>Loveleen Kaur<//Name><time>1499571077480</time><rate>4< /rate>< text>
Came here on a Friday afternoon - the lunch rush was just ending. It was open seating - you could sit in bar area or in the seating tables. We chose the seating tables since most of the bar tables are long in length but short in width. Overall, the customer service was good and knowledgeable about the menu. They helped us by making recommendations on popular dishes and tried to narrow down our taste preferences. Eventually, we went with Cauliflower Bites and going half and half on the pizza. We got half Margerita and half BBQ Chicken on the pizza. I definitely loved the Sriracha Cauliflower Bites as it covered my hot wings craving. The chicken on the BBQ pizza lacked flavor but Margerita pizza was good. It is definitely a good place to eat for some "healthier" alternatives to comfort food. Would come here again!</text>
